    method local
    case-sensitive-names
    no login-uniqueness
    no relogin-after-password-change
    one-time-password email-format plain-text
    one-time-password format characters
    one-time-password length min 10 max 10
    auth-page-timeout 1
    browser-redirect-via interface-ip
    http-redirect-after-login
    no policy-banner
    no policy-banner content
    inactivity-timeout 15
    no prevent-inactivity-logout service
    no log-user-name originating-externally
    no log-user-name other-unidentified
    log-user-name sso-fail "Unknown (SSO failed)"
    log-user-name bypass-sso "Unknown (SSO bypassed)"
    user-connections-logout inactivity authentication keep-alive
    user-connections-logout inactivity other keep-alive
    user-connections-logout reported authentication terminate
    user-connections-logout reported other terminate after 15
    inactive-user login
    inactive-user timeout
    age-out 60
    show-user-status-window
    disconnected-user-detect
    status-window-heartbeat period 120
    status-window-heartbeat timeout 10
    no open-in-same-window
    web-login-session-limit 30

    acceptable-use-policy
        window-size 460 310
        scroll-bars
        no content
        aup-on-zones trusted
        no aup-on-zones wan
        aup-on-zones public
        no aup-on-zones wireless
        no aup-on-zones vpn
        exit

    no customize-login-page preempt
    no customize-login-page authentication
    no customize-login-page logged-out
    no customize-login-page full
    no customize-login-page disallowed
    no customize-login-page lockout
    no customize-login-page status
    no customize-login-page guest-status
    no customize-login-page access-barred
    no customize-login-page access-down
    no customize-login-page access-unavailable

    exit
